# FIXLOG ‚Äî every fix, its proof, and its regression status

Process (Vinay, 2026-06-12): every fix lands here with a regression guard.
After EVERY new fix: (1) run the full suite ‚Äî all guards below must stay
green; (2) re-check any ‚öÝ manual items touched by the change. Step-by-step
upgrades, nothing previously fixed may silently break.

Legend: ‚úÖ automated regression test ¬∑ ‚öÝ manual check (no automated guard yet)
